Rig Veda talks about\nriver Ganges only once. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mpyQkddNB2w/UBtai6HLReI/AAAAAAAAPKU/t4pvP0MGZxc/s1600/imagesCA3SGLQ5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"261\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mpyQkddNB2w/UBtai6HLReI/AAAAAAAAPKU/t4pvP0MGZxc/s320/imagesCA3SGLQ5.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Read my post MOTHER OF\nALL CIVILIZATIONS- VADAKAYIL. Krisha\u2019s brother Balarama describes the drying up\nriver , as he walks down the banks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-i20CwGUxi4w/UBtazrmmzfI/AAAAAAAAPKs/70prZDP9Zac/s1600/imagesCAITD0HQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-i20CwGUxi4w/UBtazrmmzfI/AAAAAAAAPKs/70prZDP9Zac/s400/imagesCAITD0HQ.jpg\" width=\"352\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are several\ncharacters who are common both to Ramayana and Mahabharata. Hanuman and Bhima\nas both Vayu\u2019s children. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Hanuman belongs to Ramayana while Bhima and his\nwife Draupadi belongs to Mahabharata. An old Hanuman told Bhima ( searching for\na flower for Draupadi ) who was vain about his great strength to lift his tail\nand Bhima could not. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C4jtIyvq5AU/UBta877ofAI/AAAAAAAAPK0/MfIp3XEOkpg/s1600/imagesCAAZK11F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-C4jtIyvq5AU/UBta877ofAI/AAAAAAAAPK0/MfIp3XEOkpg/s320/imagesCAAZK11F.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In addition there are\nseveral other characters common to both epics, like Narada,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Durvasha Muni , Parashurama ( who can live as\nlong as he wants ) etc. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Those days people\nlived for more than 180 years. The Maharishis with 12 strand DNA lived much\nlonger.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MbmavnMZxJk/UBtbDPOXP-I/AAAAAAAAPK8/SnWcUireMvQ/s1600/imagesCADHILZY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Yugas have been\nfudged by the translating West, who wanted to throw a cloud.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7pT7izGvno0/UBtncBdZ64I/AAAAAAAAPQ4/G4iC1-Mk6OU/s1600/imagesCAJR6BRI.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"228\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7pT7izGvno0/UBtncBdZ64I/AAAAAAAAPQ4/G4iC1-Mk6OU/s320/imagesCAJR6BRI.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vasishtha\u2019s son Sakthi,\nhad a son called Parasara and Parasara\u2019s son was Veda Vyasa, who wrote the\nMahabharata . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>So this means Vasishtha\nwas the great grandfather of Vyasa. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Brahmarshi\nVasishtha lived from the time of Satyavrata Manu, to the time of Sri Rama. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Sri Rama was Vasistha\u2019s student. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-O9iyxD1nQbc/UBtbJkY2luI/AAAAAAAAPLE/9oOcPUZ8FHw/s1600/imagesCAN2D802.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-O9iyxD1nQbc/UBtbJkY2luI/AAAAAAAAPLE/9oOcPUZ8FHw/s1600/imagesCAN2D802.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lord Krishna was named\nby Garga, the son of Bharadwaja, who was quoted by Parasara in the Brihat Parasara\nHora Sastra. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Viswamitra the Guru of Lord\nRama\u2019s teacher was the grand \u2013uncle of Parashurama. Viswamitra\u2019s sister,\nSatyavati, was the grandmother of Parasurama. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Kj3cZFKWOA0/UBtnTHndmDI/AAAAAAAAPQw/MMovXIwyO_A/s1600/imagesCAG0HBAY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Kj3cZFKWOA0/UBtnTHndmDI/AAAAAAAAPQw/MMovXIwyO_A/s400/imagesCAG0HBAY.jpg\" width=\"277\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">So Viswamitra was the grand-uncle\nof Parasurama. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Young Viswamitra and\nVasishtha had once fought with each other. . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-EmAPFP7q6Jk/UBtbPKHQRGI/AAAAAAAAPLM/YEPdmnKY0lE/s1600/imagesCA2Z86FU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-EmAPFP7q6Jk/UBtbPKHQRGI/AAAAAAAAPLM/YEPdmnKY0lE/s1600/imagesCA2Z86FU.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Parasurama who fought\nwith Kshatriya kings had spared the life of Dasaratha, the father of Lord Rama.\n. At Sri Rama\u2019s wedding, Parasurama challenged him to hold the bow of Lord Vishnu\u2014the\n<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Chapam. . Parasurama killed Karthavirya\nArjuna, who had <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>defeated Ravana. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SotT2QXZJNc/UBtbcFl74DI/AAAAAAAAPLU/ICuGmEfguPo/s1600/imagesCAUF2LTJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"145\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SotT2QXZJNc/UBtbcFl74DI/AAAAAAAAPLU/ICuGmEfguPo/s320/imagesCAUF2LTJ.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Maya Danava who build\nthe Indraprasta palace hall for Yuddhistira was Ravana\u2019s father in law. .\nParasurama gave his axe to Drona. Drona was the Guru of Vyasa\u2019s grandchildren,\nthe Kauravas and the Pandavas. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-bkwrdGmYfEE/UBtbkzM5XLI/AAAAAAAAPLc/28RzjJ80O20/s1600/imagesCAXJ1WON.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Drona\u2019s father was the Maharishi\nBharadwaja, who was the pupil of Valmiki, who wrote Ramayana. . </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%;\">Valmiki was a\nfriend of King Dasaratha, the father of Lord Rama.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_wWQT1B3xaw/UBtbroczeII/AAAAAAAAPLk/NBVp9KXGF8E/s1600/imagesCAA635QP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Drona\u2019s father was Bharadwaja.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1cCkf_InIfE/UBthjeguepI/AAAAAAAAPN8/jrrpS-MZNFk/s1600/imagesCARGHPNG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; (Padma\nPuranam). Since Sri Rama and Ravana fought each other in Ramayana , this means Bhishma\nof Mahabharata was of the same generation as Lord Rama.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; The Katha Upanishad is just\na conversation between Gauthama\u2019s great grand son Nachiketas and Mrtyu (the god\nof death). Naachiketas was of Drona\u2019s generation. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Z00XYX7YqR0/UBte4srUlFI/AAAAAAAAPM8/nPuJYSFMwfk/s1600/imagesCAJ6EPAC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Z00XYX7YqR0/UBte4srUlFI/AAAAAAAAPM8/nPuJYSFMwfk/s320/imagesCAJ6EPAC.jpg\" width=\"218\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The meaning of the word\nUpanishad is to sit nearby. In the Upanishads we get a glimpse into the\nworkings of the minds of the great Indian thinkers who were unhampered by the\ntyranny of religious dogma, political authority, pressure of public opinion,\nseeking truth with single-minded devotion, rare in the history of thought.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3otFgdoN8bk/UBtdVTJmGaI/AAAAAAAAPMc/Ej1XdkiFIVg/s1600/imagesCAEO1RVP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"198\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3otFgdoN8bk/UBtdVTJmGaI/AAAAAAAAPMc/Ej1XdkiFIVg/s320/imagesCAEO1RVP.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Balarama, the brother\nof Lord Krishna, visited King Janaka, Rama\u2019s wife Sita\u2019s father. He trained\nDuryodhana in Gada Yuddha ( battle with the heavy mace club) at Mithila..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\nI can take this post to 50 pages-- it is NOT worth it.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">(Srimad-Bhagavatam First Canto, Chapter 3, text 24)\n<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Here's the account from the \"Ramayana\" of Sage\nValmiki about the construction of Ram Sethu bridge 30 kilometers long : <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">\"At Rama's command, those lions among the monkeys\nentered the mighty forest with alacrity in hundreds and thousands on every side\nand those leaders on the simian tribes, tearing up the rocks, which in size\nthey resembled, and the trees also dragged them to the sea and they covered the\nocean with Sala, Ashvararna, (list of tree names).Those foremost monkeys\ntransported those trees, with or without roots, bearing them like so many standards\nof Indra (the king of heaven) and they heaped (list of tree names) here and\nthere. With the aid of mechanical devices, those powerful colossi dug up stones\nas big as elephants and rocks, and the water suddenly spouted into the air only\nto fall instantly. Thereafter those monkeys churned up the sea by rushing into\nit on all sides pulling on the chains. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-K0TpZeH-XXQ/UBzNGMdyEgI/AAAAAAAAPSY/V7H-P8APIOg/s1600/imagesCAUCFUTX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; it was by hundreds and thousands that those monkeys, like unto giants, made\nuse of reeds, logs and blossoming trees to construct that bridge, rushing\nhither and thither with blocks of stone resembling mountains or the peaks of\ncrags, which, flung into the sea, fell with a resounding crash. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q3rTnxjCsKs/UBzNMpQfidI/AAAAAAAAPSg/cB_HrusZf4Q/s1600/imagesCAJAYUFZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"276\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q3rTnxjCsKs/UBzNMpQfidI/AAAAAAAAPSg/cB_HrusZf4Q/s400/imagesCAJAYUFZ.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">\"The first day those monkeys resembling elephants,\nor immense energy, full of high spirits and exceedingly merry, erected fourteen\nleagues of masonry. The second day, those highly active monkeys of formidable\nstature set up twenty leagues. Bestirring themselves, those giants threw\ntwenty-one leagues of structure over the ocean on the third day and on the\nfourth, working feverishly, they built up twenty-two leagues in extent. The\nfifth day, those monkeys, industrious workers, reached to twenty-three leagues\ndistance from the further shore. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EDXJeMtyQnk/UBzNZMSIU-I/AAAAAAAAPSw/sQZbxXf2obU/s1600/imagesCA3CSR7E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EDXJeMtyQnk/UBzNZMSIU-I/AAAAAAAAPSw/sQZbxXf2obU/s400/imagesCA3CSR7E.jpg\" width=\"299\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">\"Those monkeys thereafter dived, swam and shouted at\nthe sight of that unimaginable marvel that was almost inconceivable and caused\none to tremble! And all beings beheld that causeway thrown over the ocean and\nby hundreds and thousands of kotis (millions), those monkeys, full of valor,\nhaving built that bridge over the immense repository of waters, reached the\nopposite shore. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OB4FdUog0Sc/UBzNfmRRhKI/AAAAAAAAPS4/KvyMKloziWg/s1600/imagesCAM8ZYJG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OB4FdUog0Sc/UBzNfmRRhKI/AAAAAAAAPS4/KvyMKloziWg/s400/imagesCAM8ZYJG.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: #0070c0;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">\"Vast, well-constructed, magnificent with its\nwonderful paved floor, solidly cemented, that great causeway like unto a line\ntraced on the waves, resembled the parting of a woman's hair. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Here is a\nconversion:&nbsp;</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">A yojanas is 8000 Dhanus/bows and each bow is 6 feet&nbsp;</span><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">A nimesa is 16/73 of a second, as deduced from the following\nin the Purans:&nbsp;</span><o:p><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">&nbsp;</span></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">15 nimesa = 1 Kastha <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">30 Kastha = 1 Kala <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">30 Kala = 1 Mahutra <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">30 Malhutra = 1 day and night </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">If we convert them to their equivalent modern units, where\neach yojanas is 9 miles and each nimesha is 16/73.3 seconds, substituting it\ninto the speed of the sun by the Rig Veda gives the speed of the sun as 186,536\nmiles per second. The most accurate figure for the speed of light as of today\nis 186,282 miles per second. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">This means the Rig Veda figure is 99% accurate to the modern\nfigure. This kind of accuracy can only be achieved with laser technology and highly\nsophisticated measuring equipment. However, this just corroborates what we\nalready know from the Vymanika Shastra, that they did indeed have laser\ntechnology. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\nBut according to our Queen bee, we Indians are stupid-- mind you, only Hindus.. EHV\ntransformers are custom designed for each installation and are made to order,\nweighing as much as 300 tons each, and must be in stock. The PM and Defence\nMinister must be involved in this inventory. India must make our own EHV\ntransformers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uKdYwZMSJoM/UBli0AThdlI/AAAAAAAAO8k/WqVCkks_euk/s1600/untitledcccc.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uKdYwZMSJoM/UBli0AThdlI/AAAAAAAAO8k/WqVCkks_euk/s400/untitledcccc.png\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Long term preventative\nmeasures must be charted to protect against Coronal Mass Ejections, ( and also\nmilitary attack EMPs ) including digging transmission cables into the soil,\nplacing lightning rods on transmission wires, reducing the operating voltages of\ntransformers, and using cables that are shorter than 10 kilometers. It might\nalso be possible to develop and deploy large resistors that would add another\nlevel of protection to large transformers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Society's dependence on\ngadgets leaves our way of life vulnerable to space weather.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Till India has the\ntechnology to<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>predict such solar storm,\nit is better to shield<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the electrical\ngrid by shutting off power to some of the vulnerable areas having nuclear\nplants ,military communication units, until the danger passes. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9dRR2QC-hbw/UBli8LOPyyI/AAAAAAAAO8s/qBZNIcyodR8/s1600/untitledzxxc.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"240\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9dRR2QC-hbw/UBli8LOPyyI/AAAAAAAAO8s/qBZNIcyodR8/s320/untitledzxxc.png\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the nuclear\nfacility\u2019s backup generators either fail to start, or run out of fuel, the\nreactor cores will start to melt down. After a few days without electricity to\nrun the cooling system pumps, the water bath covering the spent fuel rods\nstored in \u201cspent fuel ponds\u201d will boil away, allowing the stored fuel rods to\nmelt down and burn . Since the Nuclear Regulatory Commission (NRC) currently\nmandates that only one week\u2019s supply of backup generator fuel needs to be\nstored at each reactor site, it is likely that after we witness the spectacular\nnight-time celestial light show from the next extreme GMD we will have about\none week in which to prepare ourselves for Armageddon.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">India must start making\nThorium Nuclear plants to reduce this danger. I am NOT being ahead of our times\nhere.\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Since India has the\nworlds best Thorium reserves, theWest is tripping over each other to offer us\nOBSELETE Uranium powered nuclear reactors. Thorium contains 150 times more\nenergy than Uranium and is the MOST efficient combustible. Since Thorium is\nonly slightly radio active , it is clean with no burden of nuclear waste\ndisposal. . A thorium-powered reactor is inherently safe. It doesn't run the\nrisk of \"meltdown\" or explosion nor can even a dirty bomb be created.\nIts nuclear reaction simply stops when its neutron exciter is turned off.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I4x2vcBDAJ8/UBln8_rPkZI/AAAAAAAAO-U/oT1sxfqh4e4/s1600/imagesCASPF1X2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"276\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I4x2vcBDAJ8/UBln8_rPkZI/AAAAAAAAO-U/oT1sxfqh4e4/s320/imagesCASPF1X2.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Think of an EMP as a\nsuper-powerful radio wave capable of inducing damaging voltage spikes in\nelectrical wires and electronic devices across vast geographical areas. What is\ngenerally referred to as an EMP strike is the deliberate detonation of a\nnuclear device at a high altitude, roughly defined as somewhere 40 and 400\nkilometers above the surface of the earth. Nuclear detonations of this type\nhave the potential to cause serious damage to electronics and electrical power\ngrids along their line of sight, covering huge distances on the order of a\ncircular area 2,500 kilometers in diameter.The geomagnetic effects of extreme\nsolar storms are sometimes also described as a \u201cnatural EMP\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VtwZDlXquzo/UBlbtpwBFDI/AAAAAAAAO6M/sbOc11M8lvc/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"271\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VtwZDlXquzo/UBlbtpwBFDI/AAAAAAAAO6M/sbOc11M8lvc/s400/images.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">An<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>EMP attack would also cause widespread grid\ncollapse. A powerful<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>EMP<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>from a sub-orbital nuclear detonation would\ncause extreme electromagnetic effects, starting with an initial short duration\n\u201cspeed of light\u201d pulse, referred to as an \u201cE1\u201d effect, followed by a middle duration\npulse called an \u201cE2\u201d effect, which is followed by a longer duration disturbance\nknown as an \u201cE3\u201d effect. The \u201cE1\u201d effect lasts on the order of a few\nnanoseconds.The intermediate \u201cE2\u201d effects last a fraction of a second <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the case of a\nnuclear induced EMP, its E3 effect starts after about a half second and may\ncontinue for several minutes. The E3 effect can be thought of as a \u201clong slow\nburn\u201d, and electromagnetically it is quite similar to the effects from an\nextreme GMD. The main difference between the E3 from an EMP and what occurs\nduring an extreme GMD is that the EMP effect may continue for<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>a number of minutes, whereas the extreme GMD\nmay continue for a number of hours or days. However, the magnitude of the\ninduced magnetic field strengths from an EMP attack and an extreme GMD are\nabout the same, with similar potential for causing severe damage to EHV\ntransformers across the affected areas.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2SiBJ99Lsro/UBljD_xg14I/AAAAAAAAO80/Z7tjToziV6I/s1600/imagesCAC7G7B6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"221\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2SiBJ99Lsro/UBljD_xg14I/AAAAAAAAO80/Z7tjToziV6I/s400/imagesCAC7G7B6.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Inside the affected\narea, an EMP\u2019s E3 effect would cause a similar degree of damage to the EHV\ntransformers as that from an extreme GMD, but the E1 and E2 effects would cause\nfar greater damage to electronic control systems than that from a GMD of\nsimilar intensity. Contrary to popular opinion, most personal electronic\ndevices would probably survive with little or no damage, especially if they\nwere not turned on at the moment of EMP, as would most automobiles. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">However,\nmost complex electronic systems that contained digital microchips in\ncombination with long runs of Ethernet cables (or other interconnecting\ncabling) which act like antennas for receiving EMP induced voltage spikes,\nwould experience nearly 100% failure.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\n</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FHDUbUmPUBc/UBlXrSpnSeI/AAAAAAAAO30/LQUIT_uJUCQ/s1600/xxxz.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"284\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FHDUbUmPUBc/UBlXrSpnSeI/AAAAAAAAO30/LQUIT_uJUCQ/s400/xxxz.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A \u201csuccessful\u201d EMP attack launched would result in the immediate collapse of the power grid, and crash the stock market.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p> </o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">We must have backup generators, inside EMP-hardened steel containers to be available for quick change-out in the event that any of these items were damaged by an EMP or GMD. </span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">High-voltage transformers must be directly connected to the ground to neutralize power surges from lightning strikes and other transient phenomen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Hns1WrL-jlI/UBlX8jQJWtI/AAAAAAAAO4E/Df6JlKqVBWs/s1600/400px-Magnetosphere_rendition.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"175\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Hns1WrL-jlI/UBlX8jQJWtI/AAAAAAAAO4E/Df6JlKqVBWs/s320/400px-Magnetosphere_rendition.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Modern digital automatic electronic control systems are highly susceptible to damage from EMP. These systems include programmable logic controllers (PLC), digital control systems (DCS),<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">  </span>and supervisory control and data acquisition systems (SCADA), all of which are absolutely critical for running factories, refineries, power plants, nuclear reactors, sewage plants, etc., as well as for diagnosing problems.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>This is why on our ships we do NOT do any welding without a return current cable. It is prevent corruption damage to PLCs and microprocessors -- NOT to prevent fires .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/L4IOOkekW6M/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/L4IOOkekW6M&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/L4IOOkekW6M&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Not preparing for this scenario can result in such terrible<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>suffering, death, and environmental destruction on a scale not seen since the extinction of the dinosaurs some 65 million years ago.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The vulnerability of both the grid and modern microelectronics to debilitating damage from severe electromagnetic disturbances and<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>electromagnetic pulse (EMP) resulting from the deliberate detonation of a nuclear device at a high altitude above the earth, must be taken most seriously.. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "13", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/565659882070636042/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6168106782307350288", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-07-31T14:31:00+05:30", "updated": "2013-09-03T11:30:33+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzc4MTg4MDMzNzM0Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/07/my-experience-at-mundra-port-adani-sez.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6168106782307350288", "title": "MY EXPERIENCE AT MUNDRA PORT , ADANI SEZ-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong><span style=\"color: red;\">MUNDRA PORT, &nbsp;ADANI PORT AND SPECIAL ECONOMIC ZONE , &nbsp; SEZ</span> -&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</strong></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XkniCIQEZyQ/UBeePrgHmdI/AAAAAAAAOws/qpjz1P-LNCU/s1600/XXXX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"172\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XkniCIQEZyQ/UBeePrgHmdI/AAAAAAAAOws/qpjz1P-LNCU/s400/XXXX.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nEarly this year ( 2012 ) my chemical tanker laden with Methanol from Sohar Oman went to Mundra Port Gujarat for discharge.<br />\n<br />\nI had a bizarre experience there,&nbsp; never experienced before in my 3 decades of command.<br />\n<br />\nThe Methanol at Sohar was loaded under absolute quality control. <br />\n<br />\nMy ship's stainless steel tanks failed the PTT test of wall wash. It was a expensive first foot failure for Capt Vadakayil--for the first time in his life.<br />\n<br />\nSince I always back myself in such bad situations, I&nbsp; gave a rare challenge.&nbsp; I contested the Lab report and called in my P&amp;I insurers from London.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nYou can read about this by punching into Google search--<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><strong>&nbsp;WALL WASH PTT WITHOUT TEARS, CHEMICAL TANKERS- VADAKAYIL.</strong></span>&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nBelieve me when I say &nbsp;taking on a shore wall wash lab is always a losing battle. <br />\n<br />\nTo cut a long story short, I won. <br />\n<br />\nThe lab would be put to an strict inspection for vetting their own competence and procedures.<br />\n<br />\nSo we went hoppety hop to Mundra Port to discharge this stuff.&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nThough my VLCC where I was second mate was the first to discharge at Vadinar SBM terminal and I was engaged in lighterage operations at Sikka , where I commanded mother ships discharging into daughter vessels, later on I lost touch with Gujarat. &nbsp;I was coming to Gujarat after probably 2 decades.<br />\n<br />\nOf course I used to remember Gujarat. <br />\n<br />\nWe used to go ashore by launch and at low tide the boat had to stop way off the shore. We used to ride piggy back on young guys for a small fee, who would wade through mud and carry us on their backsides till our feet could touch terra firma. And at this time I could see conch shells ( Shank ) as big as large coconuts.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WirYKcVr7tA/UBeje7dzszI/AAAAAAAAOyk/IKzkkYwlX1I/s1600/imagesCACUQ4VX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"241\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WirYKcVr7tA/UBeje7dzszI/AAAAAAAAOyk/IKzkkYwlX1I/s400/imagesCACUQ4VX.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn the evenings, invariably the daughter ship Captain ,would come on my ship with his family and the Loading master, by crane basket transfer , &nbsp;to chat over a few beers and have dinner. My wife used to play host . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oovaM0hqZ1A/UBejwsEuDuI/AAAAAAAAOys/7rp9W8jBfC0/s1600/ffff.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oovaM0hqZ1A/UBejwsEuDuI/AAAAAAAAOys/7rp9W8jBfC0/s320/ffff.png\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMother ships had bond ( booze ) while daughter ships were coastal and were devoid of bond.<br />\n<br />\nWe used to buy large crabs, from fishing boats who came alongside , clean them up and put them in a hundi , with just salt at the bottom and steam them. No water was put. The crabs stewed in their own juices. The flesh of the extraordinary large crabs used to be so tasty. <br />\n<br />\nToday with the rape of the ecology by mindless sanctions of development-- all this marine ecology has disappeared. Rich mangroves forest areas have been choked. The Gujarat fishermen now have to venture into the Pakistani waters and poach in case they have to make&nbsp;a profit.&nbsp; Is this the cost of development?<br />\n<br />\nI don't want to take names here.<br />\n<br />\nAs a patriotic Indian I was proud after reading about Gautam Adani's initiative and the great strides he had made in starting&nbsp;such a fantastic port, from marshland. Mundra Port&nbsp;was the largest among 12 private ports of India. <br />\n<br />\nThe first bad taste came when the agents send a email stating that unless I waive all my rights away, i cannot berth at Mundra Port-- and that every ship till now has signed such a waiver. <br />\n<br />\nMy ship had to berth on 100 % terms of Mundra Port, come hell , come high water. &nbsp;I have never seen such a legal document like this, ever before.<br />\n<br />\nNaturally I had to refer this to my&nbsp;owners in Japan and my Managers in Singapore.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nMy charterers in USA&nbsp;, was quick in imploring that I should sign this waiver as soon as possible. To cut a long story short, I was forced to sign this, against my better judgement on being advised to do so by the owners of the ship.<br />\n<br />\nBetween the time&nbsp;the pilot boarded to berth the ship and the time I dropped off the outgoing pilot, after discharging all the Methanol, Mundra port became my least favourite&nbsp;port among the all the ports of this planet.<br />\n<br />\nFirst of all my ship was berthed at a unsafe coal jetty, with trucks and cars driving past, and at least 2 dozen people on the quay using their mobile phones. <br />\n<br />\nThere was NOT a single employee, port official (like Customs/Immigration etc) &nbsp;or a service provider in the port, who did NOT curse&nbsp;Adani Inc under his breath. <br />\n<br />\nIt left me wondering -what the hell, are these guys jealous of a young successful Indian entrepreneur Gautam Adani , when actually they should be proud of him ?<br />\n<br />\nThey all gave me unsolicited information that Gautam Adani was a pauper who rose up to dizzying heights not because of his brains , but because of his wheeling and dealing.<br />\n<br />\nOne of his own school mates at CN Seth Vidyalaya&nbsp;told me about young Gautam Adani . That he was from a impoverished family, and that he lacked the grey matter in class etc.<br />\n<br />\nAgain I told myself-- sheer jealousy.<br />\n<br />\nBut then could everybody be wrong? <br />\n<br />\nSo I challenged this man to authenticate his charges. <br />\n<br />\nSo he says&nbsp; 'The whole of Gujarat knows that all this land of area 14500 acres or 5.8 crore square metres of land has been given to him for single digit rupee cost -- without auction !\"<br />\n<br />\nTo be frank I was a bit shocked.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nIf so how is that nobody has filed a complaint? Surely some business rival should&nbsp;take him on?&nbsp; Are we not in the age of Anna Hazare?<br />\n<br />\nSuddenly my Peruvian Chief Officer calls me up on walkie talkie and says \"&nbsp; Sir, the cargo &nbsp;tank surveyors are opening out the tanks domes to do open sampling. If we do NOT start cargo within 2 hours of coming alongside ( not gangway down ). there will be some thousand US dollars fine for the next minute and then every hour after that\"<br />\n<br />\nTo add to our woes dozens of labourers were tipping coal from the empty chutes and I had a fine layer of black coal all over my grey deck, including my nostrils.<br />\n<br />\nMethanol is such a clean cargo, that you cant even have a speck of dust in the cargo.<br />\n<br />\nI tried to expostulate, being an Indian , I did NOT want to make an issue in an Indian port, if things could be reasoned out amicably.<br />\n<br />\nThis is when I notices the arrogance of the port. Never seen anything like thing before in any other port in the world.&nbsp; They stopped the tipping , when I said I will inform the buyers or Methanol, within an hour.<br />\n<br />\nThe top managers of the port ( no names!) , punch drunk with&nbsp;power, were absolutely sure of themselves. <em><span style=\"color: red;\">&nbsp;\" This is our way, If you don't like it you can cast off your ship on your account and drop anchor!&nbsp; If the other ship on the next berth can do open ullaging ( Indian SCI ship with diesel ) , why cant you do it? \"</span></em><br />\n<br />\nThey made a big mistake. <br />\n<br />\nThey were cocky enough and gave this in writing by email via the agents. Which I promptly forwarded to my P&amp;I in London.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nSurely Mundra -- nay Adani port is NOT gonna get any awards in the near future-- like how they wrangled the \"BEST PORT OF THE YEAR AWARD 2006\" from Lloyds London.<br />\n<br />\nThe Adani brand had taken a huge dent because of this incident, in the foreign shipping circles.&nbsp; Never mind their local clout!<br />\n<br />\nTrying to rush cargo surveyors to do open ullaging on 28 nos SS tanks full of Methanol, is so dangerous --in fact more dangerous than putting a cobra in your only child's bedroom and locking the door.<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">14500 acres or 5.8 crore square metres of land bought for&nbsp;single digit rupee cost per sq metre -- without auction, in the year 2003 - </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">WOW !</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">-- if this is NOT wheeling and dealin' and favouritism , what else could it be?</span> </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VHNtbNDfxjU/UBem0hhFFiI/AAAAAAAAO1s/p4BxdJAcImY/s1600/narendra.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"267\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VHNtbNDfxjU/UBem0hhFFiI/AAAAAAAAO1s/p4BxdJAcImY/s400/narendra.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAnd we have put poor Raja in jail. <br />\n<br />\n<em>In USA lobbyists are official pimps who do the wheeling -dealin' and bribery.&nbsp; </em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The CBI had 5,851 recordings\nof \u201cwheeling and dealing\u201d <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>phone\nconversations by Nira Radia Radia, some of which clearly outline Radia's attempts to\nbroker deals in relation to the 2G spectrum sale. The tapes demonstrate how\nRadia attempted to powerful media persons to influence the decision to appoint A. Raja\nas telecom minister. She was Ratan Tata\u2019s lobbyist. <o:p></o:p></span></em><br />\n<br />\n<br />\nPunch into google search <strong><span style=\"color: blue;\">PERSONAL BRANDING- VADAKAYIL</span></strong>.<br />\n<br />\nTop managers of ports must care about not denting their own brand. If Gautam Adani reads this post, he must bear this in mind. <br />\n<br />\nGautam Adani was in the first floor restaurant Chambers of Taj hotel Mumbai when Paki terrorists attacked -- and he was rescued after 2 hours by commandos.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rflin4OzanU/UBn5eqsDNlI/AAAAAAAAPEA/DgszH6D9kNs/s1600/imagesCA85UYSU.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rflin4OzanU/UBn5eqsDNlI/AAAAAAAAPEA/DgszH6D9kNs/s320/imagesCA85UYSU.jpg\" width=\"292\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAt Mundra port if the Captain does NOT meet the corrupt gratuity demands ( excessive ) of the boarding customs officer on arival , he can forget about receiving provisions and stores.&nbsp; Customs have been given unlimited powers quoting LEVEL 2&nbsp; security.&nbsp; And finally the Captain has waived all his powers to this private port.<br />\n<br />\nSo, from now on anybody who punches ito Google search MUNDRA PORT EXPERIENCE , will see this post on page one among thousands-- such is the readership I command.<br />\n<br />\nWhen Mundra port's top bosses send a&nbsp;communication to a senior Indian Master , Capt Vadakayil, telling him to FU#K OFF,&nbsp; they never anticipated this permanent dent in their brand, right?<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Grace and peace!</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/E-amYtG_3so/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/E-amYtG_3so&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/E-amYtG_3so&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xyY6yXVp1kc/UBSRcXx9V2I/AAAAAAAAOaY/X_eJj4T5REI/s1600/lajpat-rai.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xyY6yXVp1kc/UBSRcXx9V2I/AAAAAAAAOaY/X_eJj4T5REI/s640/lajpat-rai.jpg\" width=\"414\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong><span style=\"color: blue;\">THE FREEDOM FIGHTER , A\nMARTYR WHO FELT FOR HIS MOTHERLAND-&nbsp; CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></strong></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nearly 4 decades ago, when\nI did my 2nd Mate's exam, we used to go to Shere-e Punjab restaurant from\nSeaman's Club Mumbai , to have our dinner. It was a economy hotel , but gave\ngood food and fast service--and we could ill affors to lose time waiting for service.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I asked my Punjabi\nbatch mate, what does the name of the restaurant indicate. He had NO dang clue. </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Well\nLala Lajpat Rai, is the LION of Punjab.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It must be noted that in\n1857, during the First war of Independence, the whole of India united as one to\ndrive away the British. The Sikhs and the Gurkhas sided with the British.\nGurkhas are NOT Indians.&nbsp; Sikhs must know that this is a permanent blot on their\nfair name.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The 1857, Sepoy Mutiny\nwas engineered by Rothschild, the German Jewish owners of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>British East India Company. They had their\npaid Indian \"double agent\" stooges , taunting the Hindu and Muslim\nsoldiers,&nbsp; that they are \"dharm bhrasht\", and that the lard of cow\nand pig fat was used on the cartridges they were forced to bite off. &nbsp;This constant nit-pickin' did the trick.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This\nrevolt was carefully nurtured and allowed to fan out, in a controlled manner,\nso that Rothschild who onwed the British East India Company could stop all pretences of being traders, and now take over the British\nEmpire in India.&nbsp; The first thing they did was to have a huge party at the Red\nFort, and prise off the golden spires of Taj Mahal, melt it and cart it away to\ntheir underground bank vaults.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Same way, Lala Lajpat\nRai was done in by heavy Lathi blows on the left side of his chest. The British\nknew very well&nbsp;that he had a heart condition, as he had been imprisoned by them several\ntimes, in horrible conditions. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lala Lajpat Rai was\nleading a peaceful and silent demonstration, the way Mahatma Gandhi wanted it,\noutside Lahore Railway station, on Oct 30th 1928.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>He was standing behind the first row of\nbarbed wire, along with Pandit madan Mohan Malivya.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; The other side had paid Indian stooges welcoming Simon and party--BR Ambedkar was such a British agent..&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">Lala&nbsp;</span>was beaten up for no plausible reason.\n Bhagat Singh was eye witness, as he was part of this group of protestors. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Though in severe pain,\nthe same evening Lala told at a crowded public meeting in Lahore City,\n\"Every blow on our bodies this afternoon is like a nail driven into the\ncoffin of British imperialism.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">17 days later, on Nov\n17th , Lala Lajpat Rai, succumbed to the shock of the internal injury suffered.\nDr. Lt Col Roy, who had examined Lala 5 hours before the arrival of Simon\nCommission at Lahore, had recorded that his chest on the left side was swollen\nand had red welt marks, with severe pain while breathing. </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nov 17th is\ncelebrated by Martyr's day in India. Every Indian must know what this day\nmeans.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The British were equal\nto the occasion. The attributed the blue marks on the left side of the chest on\nthe dead body of Lala as chicanery by the Indians , who used blue INK , and\nmade marks.&nbsp; Professor Abdul Majid Khan was roped in to announce on Radio\nJullunder that he personally witnessed the scene and that no blows were\nreceived by Lala Lajpat Rai at all on his body. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The British bribed another\nIndian to announce that these ink marks were put on the advise of S Kishen\nSingh, the father of Bhagat Singh to Achint Ram, and that a&nbsp;photographer was\ntold to take these doctored pictures, for political leverage.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bhagat Singh who was a\ngraduate from the National College Lahore, founded by Lala, was emotionally\ncharged on hearing this, &nbsp;to take revenge--.and he did!</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
