He understands\nmusic.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xl7bVOSHtw4/UBN4_8X-jwI/AAAAAAAAONk/ovW2Et47QNc/s1600/ab+JERRY+.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"192\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xl7bVOSHtw4/UBN4_8X-jwI/AAAAAAAAONk/ovW2Et47QNc/s200/ab+JERRY+.jpg\" width=\"200\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">..</span></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "2", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7607798083621999090/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6169217162771066470", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-07-26T12:13:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-07-26T12:13:24+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzQzMjg1MDA0NDU2Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/07/chemical-hazards-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6169217162771066470", "title": "CHEMICAL HAZARDS  ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CeP9VyrALz4/UBDmv-flu1I/AAAAAAAAOGI/5dSg1I95T_I/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CeP9VyrALz4/UBDmv-flu1I/AAAAAAAAOGI/5dSg1I95T_I/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><strong>CHEMICAL HAZARDS <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>ON CHEMICAL TANKERS- &nbsp;CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></strong></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><strong>Personal Protective Equipment</strong> - The items\nlisted are those recommended by (a) manufacturers, either in technical\nbulletins or in Material Safety Data Sheets, (b) the Chemical Manufacturers\nAssociation, or (c) the National Safety Council, for use by personnel while\nresponding to fire or accidental discharge of the chemical.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>They are intended to protect the lungs, eyes,\nand skin.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Safety showers and eyewash\nfountains are considered to be important protective equipment for the handling\nof almost all chemicals; they are not usually listed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Symptoms Following\nExposure</strong> - These are brief descriptions of the effects observed in humans when\nthe vapor (gas) is inhaled, when the liquid or solid is ingested (swallowed),\nand when the liquid or solid comes in contact with the eyes or skin.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Treatment for Exposure</strong>\n- \u201cFirst-aid\u201d procedures are recommended.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>They deal with exposure to the vapor (gas), liquid, or solid and include\ninhalation, ingestion (swallowing) and contact with eyes or skin.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The instruction \u201cDo NOT induce vomiting\u201d is\ngiven if an unusual hazard is associated with the chemical being sucked into\nthe lungs (aspiration) while the patient is vomiting.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\u201cSeek medical attention\u201d or \u201cCall a doctor\u201d\nis recommended in those cases where only competent medical personnel can treat\nthe injury properly.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>In all cases of\nhuman exposure, seek medical assistance as soon as possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Threshold Limit Value</strong> \u2013\n<strong>Time Weighted Average</strong> -The Threshold Limit Value Time Weighted Average\n(TLV-TWA) is usually expressed in units of parts per million (ppm) - i.e., the\nparts of vapor (gas) per million parts of contaminated air by volume at 25oC\n(77oF) and one atmosphere pressure.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>For\na chemical that forms a fine mist or dust, the concentration is given in\nmilligrams per cubic meter (mg/m3).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The\nTLV is defined as the concentration of the substance in air that can be\nbreathed for five consecutive eight-hour workdays (40-hour work week) by most\npeople without adverse effect (American Conference of Governmental Industrial\nHygienists, \u201cThreshold Limit Values for Substance in Workroom Air, Adopted by\nACGIH\u201d).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>As some people become ill after\nexposure to concentrations lower than the TLV, this value cannot be used to\ndefine exactly what is a \u201csafe\u201d or \u201cdangerous\u201d concentration.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">No entry appears when\nthe chemical is a mixture; it is possible to calculate the TLV for a mixture\nonly when the TLV for each component of the mixture is known and the\ncomposition of the mixture by weight is also known.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Threshold Limit Value -\nShort-Term Exposure Limits</strong> - The parts of vapor (gas per million parts of\ncontaminated air by volume at 25oC (77oF) and one atmosphere pressure is\ngiven.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The limits are given in\nmilligrams per cubic meter for chemicals that can form a fine mist or\ndust.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The values given are the maximum\npermissible average exposures for the time periods specified.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Threshold Limit Value \u2013\nCeiling Value</strong> \u2013 The parts of vapor (gas per million parts of contaminated air\nby volume at 25oC (77oF) and one atmosphere pressure is given.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The limits are given in milligrams per cubic\nmeter for chemicals that can form a fine mist or dust.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The values given are for a concentration that\nis not to be exceeded at any time.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Toxicity by Ingestion</strong> -\nThe Grade and corresponding LD50 value are those defined by the National\nAcademy of Sciences, Committee on Hazardous Materials, \u201cEvaluation of the\nHazard of Bulk Water Transportation of Industrial Chemicals, A Tentative\nGuide,\u201d Washington, D.C., 1972.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Data\nwere also collected from other sources and converted to the appropriate Grade\nbefore entry in this manual.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The term\nLD50 signifies that about 50% of the animals given the specified dose by mouth\nwill die.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Thus, for a Grade 4 chemical\n(below 50 mg/kg) the toxic dose for 50% of animals weighing 70 kg (150 lb) is\n70 X 50 = 3500 mg = 3.5 g, or less than 1 teaspoonful; it might be as little as\na few drops.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>For a Grade 1 chemical (5\nto 15g/k g), the LD50 would be between a pint and a quart for a 150-lb\nman.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>All LD50 values have been obtained\nusing small laboratory animals such as rodents, cats, and dogs.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The substantial risks taken in using these\nvalues for estimating human toxicity are the same as those taken when new drugs\nare administered to humans for the first time.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Toxicity by Inhalation</strong>\n\u2013 Similar to the Toxicity by Ingestion entry, except that the route of exposure\nis inhalation instead of ingestion.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Units and definition of units are the same.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Chronic Toxicity</strong> -\nWhere there is evidence that the chemical can cause cancer, mutagenic effects,\nteratogenic effects, or a delayed injury to vital organs such as the liver or\nkidney, a qualitative description of the effect is given.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><strong>Vapor (Gas) Irritant Characteristics</strong> - The\nmost appropriate of five statements listed below is given.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Source:<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>National Academy of Sciences, Committee on Hazardous Materials,\n\u201cEvaluation of the Hazard of Bulk Water Transportation of Industrial Chemicals,\nA Tentative Guide,\u201d Washington, D.C.,1972.)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(1) Vapors are non\nirritating to eyes and throat.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(2) Vapors cause a\nslight smarting of the eyes or respiratory system if present in high\nconcentrations.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The effect is temporary.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(3) Vapors cause\nmoderate irritation such that personnel will find high concentrations\nunpleasant.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The effect is temporary.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(4) Vapors are\nmoderately irritating such that personnel will not usually tolerate moderate or\nhigh concentrations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(5) Vapors cause severe\nirritation of eyes and throat and can cause eye and lung injury.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>They cannot be tolerated even at low\nconcentrations. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Liquid or Solid\nIrritant Characteristics</strong> - The most appropriate of the following five\nstatements is given (same source as 5.8 above):<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(1) No appreciable\nhazard.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Practically harmless to the\nskin.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(2) Minimum\nhazard.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If spilled on clothing and\nallowed to remain, may cause smarting and reddening of skin.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(3) Causes smarting of\nthe skin and first-degree burns on short exposure; may cause second-degree\nburns on long exposure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(4) Fairly severe skin\nirritant.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>May cause pain and\nsecond-degree burns after a few minutes' contact.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">(5) Severe skin\nirritant.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Causes second- and\nthird-degree burns on short contact and is very injurious to the eyes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Odor Threshold</strong> - This\nis the lowest concentration in air that most humans can detect by smell.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The value cannot be relied on to prevent over-exposure,\nbecause human sensitivity to odors varies over wide limits, some chemicals\ncannot be smelled at toxic concentrations, odors can be masked by other odors,\nand some compounds rapidly deaden the sense of smell.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>IDLH Value</strong> - The\nImmediately Dangerous to Life and Health Value - This concentration represents\na maximum level from which one could escape within 30 minutes without any\nescape-impairing symptoms or any irreversible healtheffects.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The concentrations are reported in either\nparts per million (ppm) or milligrams per cubic meter (mg/m3).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>OSHA Permissible\nExposure Limit \u2013 Time Weighted Average</strong> \u2013 Similar to the definition of the\nTLV-TWA above, except that this limit has been promulgated by the Occupational\nSafety and Health Agency.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>OSHA Permissible\nExposure Limit \u2013 Short Term Exposure Limit</strong> \u2013 Similar to the definition of the\nTVL-STEL above, except that this limit has been promulgated by the Occupational\nSafety and Health Agency.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>OSHA Permissible\nExposure Limit \u2013 Ceiling</strong> \u2013 Similar to the definition of the TVL-Ceiling above,\nexcept that this limit has been promulgated by the Occupational Safety and\nHealth Agency.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>EPA AEGL</strong> \u2013 Acute\nExposure Guideline information from the Environmental Protection Agency for the\nspecific compound listed in the manual.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Transportation of bulk\nchemicals do not only require special hardware, but also special crew training,\nboth theoretical and practical, in order for them to understand the\ncharacteristics of the various chemicals and be aware of the potential hazards\ninvolved in handling them. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Detailed hazards of\nparticular substances are provided in MSDS and in publications such as the, ICS\nTanker Safety Guide (Chemicals). The purpose of the following is to provide\nbroad guidance on these hazards, particularly those impacting on health.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><br />\n\n\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>General Hazards:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chemical cargoes may\npresent a fire hazard which will be determined by the flashpoint, boiling\npoint, flammability limits and auto-ignition temperature of the product. The\nmarine pollution hazard will be dependent on several factors that include\nbioaccumulation and the attendant risk to aquatic life or human health or\ncausing tainting to seafood. In addition, release into the marine environment\nmay cause damage to living resources, hazard to human health and consequent reduction\nof amenities.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The air pollution\nhazard posed by release into the atmosphere may be categorised by the emergency\nexposure limit (EEL) of the substance.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Health Hazards:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most of the chemicals\npresent more than one hazard to health, for example, it may:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Be corrosive.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Be poisonous.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Produce toxic\nvapours.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Pose an asphyxiation\nhazard.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Result in long-term\ndamage to eyes or the nervous system.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022 Have long-term\ncarcinogenic effects.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Toxicity:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Toxicity may be\ndescribed as the ability of a substance to cause damage to living tissue,\nimpairment of the central nervous system, severe illness or, in extreme cases,\ndeath when inhaled, ingested, or absorbed by the skin. The amounts required to\nproduce these results vary widely with the nature of the substance and the time\nof exposure to it. Toxicity is divided into two main groups; \u201cacute\u201d which\nrefers to exposure of a short duration, i.e. a single brief exposure, and the\n\u201cchronic\u201d toxicity refers to exposure of long duration, i.e. repeated or\nprolonged exposures. Toxicity is objectively evaluated on the basis of test\ndosages made on experimental animals under controlled conditions.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Prevention from\nexposures is achieved by a combination of preventing toxic fumes or liquid from\ncontaminating the workplace and the use of Personal Protective Equipment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Asphyxia:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Asphyxia can be\ndescribed as a condition caused by lack of air (oxygen) i.e. suffocation. Any\nvapour may cause asphyxiation, whether toxic or not. Danger areas are cargo\ntanks, void spaces, double bottoms, pump rooms, peaks etc. and before entering\nthese spaces The Company\u2019s Enclosed Space Entry procedures must be observed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Anesthesia:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Certain vapours have an\nanesthetic effect and may cause loss of consciousness due to its effect on the\nnervous system. Anesthetic vapours could be both toxic and non toxic.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Exposure:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Exposure may be either\nacute or chronic. With acute exposure, the victim is subjected to a one-off\nhigh level dose and the symptoms are usually immediately apparent, although\nthere can be a delayed reaction. The damage caused may be irreversible, even\nwith treatment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chronic exposure is\nassociated with a relatively low level of exposure over a period of time.\nSymptoms may not be apparent until many years later, which in some cases, could\nbe over 30 years after exposure ceases.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Exposure to the product\nmay be by inhalation, skin absorption or ingestion. Inhalation of vapour or\nmist is by far the most likely route for harmful substances to enter the body.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The effect of exposure\nwill depend upon the toxicity of the vapour, the level of contamination and the\nvolatility of the product. Exposure to the vapour may cause a variety of\neffects that could include systemic poisoning, irritation of the nose, throat\nand respiratory system and even asphyxiation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Absorption may be\ndirectly through skin contact and any physical injuries, such as cuts or\nabrasions, will serve to increase the absorption rate. Exposure may cause skin\nirritation which, in its mildest form may result in dermatitis, and systematic\neffects.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ingestion may be\ncaused, for example, by accidentally swallowing a chemical when splashed by it.\nSome liquids have corrosive properties such that if they come into contact with\nthe skin, they may completely or partly destroy living tissue, causing acute\npain. Others, although only causing slight skin irritation at the outset, can\neventually result in severe damage to the eyes and other mucous membranes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Respiratory Protection:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are various types\nof respiratory protection equipment available, ranging from simple dust masks\nto more complex types of masks. It is essential that the correct type of mask\nis worn for the specific task to be carried out.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Note that respirators\ndo not protect the user in an oxygen deficient atmosphere and they do not\nnecessarily protect against all gases that may exist on a ship. Some types of\nrespirator (filter canister type masks) are designed to protect from specific\nchemicals and are used sometimes in the petro-chemical industry ashore.\nHowever, these are not suitable for ship use and prohibited onboard Company vessels.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The only sure way that\nyou can guarantee the air you are breathing is safe, is to use a compressed air\nbreathing apparatus set filled by a dedicated compressor with a clean air\ncertificate.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Filter masks should be\nused only in areas where the air contains at least 20% by volume of oxygen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is also important to\nunderstand that a filter mask alone will not give adequate protection. It shall\nbe noted that a chemical may be both toxic and explosive/flammable.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Threshold Limit Value\n(TLV):<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">TLV refers to the\nmaximum concentration of gases, vapours, mist or sprays to which it is believed\nthat nearly all persons may be repeatedly exposed day after day without adverse\neffects. TLV is stated as Time Weighted Average (TLV-TWA), Short Term Exposure\nLimit (TLV-STEL) and Ceiling (TLV-C): usually expressed in parts per million\n(ppm). Refer to ISGOTT for more details.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Flammability:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapour given off by a\nflammable liquid will burn when ignited provided it is mixed with certain\nproportions of air. If the vapour mixture is too lean or too rich it will not\nburn. The range in which it will burn is called the flammable range, and the\nlimits are called the lower flammable limits (LFL) and the upper flammable limits\n(UFL). See definitions carried in Section 1 of these operating instructions for\nfurther details.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A flammable vapour also\nneeds Oxygen in order to burn, typically in excess of 11 percent for\nhydrocarbon vapours. In addition a flammable liquid must be at a temperature\nhigh enough to give off sufficient vapour in order to ignite (the Flash Point).\nFor the purpose of safe handling procedures, the flammability characteristics\nof various products are divided into three broad categories:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Flammable cargoes------------\nflash point not exceeding 60\u00b0C<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Combustible\ncargoes-----------flash point exceeding 60\u00b0C<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Non-combustible\ncargoes------cargoes which have no flash point<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Reactivity:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chemicals may react in\na number of ways; with water, with itself, with air, with other chemicals or\nwith other materials.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Self-reaction<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The most common form of\nself-reaction is polymerisation. Polymerisation may be a slow natural process\nwhich only degrades the product without posing any safety hazards, or it may be\na rapid exothermic reaction with a large amount of heat build-up and gases\nevolved. Such a reaction is called a run-off polymerisation and poses a serious\ndanger to both the ship and its personnel.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Products that are\nself-reactive are inhibited with a stabiliser to prevent self-reaction. The\naction to be taken in case of a polymerisation situation should be covered by\nthe ship\u2019s emergency/contingency plan.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><strong>Reaction with water<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Certain cargoes react\nwith water, most noticeable the isocyanates, in a way that could pose a danger\nto both the ship and its personnel. These cargoes are carried under inert\ncondition, see chapter 9 in the IBC code. Other cargoes react with water in a\nslow way that poses no safety hazards, but the reaction could cause chemicals\nthat may damage equipment and/or tank materials.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><strong>Reaction with air<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Certain cargoes may\nreact with air to form unstable oxygen compounds (peroxides) which, when\nallowed to build up, could cause an explosion. Such cargoes are either\ninhibited by an anti-oxidant and/or carried under inert condition.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u2022<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><strong>Reaction with other cargoes</strong> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Certain cargoes react\ndangerously with one another. Such cargoes should be stowed away from each\nother (not adjacent) and prevented from mixing by using separate cargo and vent\nlines.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The master must ensure\nthat cargoes stowed adjacent to each other are compatible, and should consult\nthe USCG CHRIS compatibility guide (Section 16) prior to loading.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Reaction with other\nmaterials:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The materials of\nconstruction must be compatible with the cargo to be carried. Some materials\nmay react with the product and trigger a self- reaction within the product,\nsome alloys will react in a non hazardous way, but render the product unusable\nor in case of an edible product, inedible. See the IBC code.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Corrositivity:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Acids, anhydrides and\nalkalis are among the most common carried corrosive substances. They can\nrapidly destroy human tissue and cause irreparable damage. They can also\ncorrode normal construction materials, and create a safety hazard to the ship.\nAcids in particular react with most metals evolving hydrogen gas, which is\nhighly flammable. As to suitable materials of construction see IBC code.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Handling of these\nsubstances should only be done wearing suitable Personal Protective Equipment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Putrefaction:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most animal and\nvegetable oils undergo decomposition, this process, known as putrefaction,\ngenerates obnoxious and toxic vapours and deplete the oxygen in the tank. Tanks\nthat have contained such product must be properly ventilated and the atmosphere\ntested prior to tank entry. This is especially important prior sending\npersonnel into the tank for sweeping purposes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Strict compliance with\nthe tank entry procedures will apply. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Coconut and Vegetable\nOils:</strong></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In addition to\nputrefaction, the above types of oil can have hazards associated with the\nproduction of Carbon Monoxide (CO). These dangers are heightened during heating\nand the final stages of discharge when CO levels have been known to reach in\nexcess of 3,000ppm. As a result, it is essential that before entering a tank\nfor either \u201csqueezing\u201d the last remaining cargo or for tank cleaning that the\nfollowing precautions are taken.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The atmosphere of the\ntanks is monitored regularly throughout discharge for the presence of CO.\nTemperatures should also be taken as excessive temperatures will assist in the\nproduction of CO.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The eight-hour safe\nexposure limit for CO is given as ,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>30PPM<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>although short-term\nexposure (15 minutes) of up to 200ppm can be allowed under exceptional\ncircumstances. CO is toxic by inhalation and can cause serious damage to heath.\nAccordingly, a meter, capable of measuring these limits, must be on board. Full\nenclosed space entry procedures as detailed in the SEM must also be followed with\nadditional checks made for CO. Failure to follow these precautions may result\nin fatalities.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>CHEMICAL REACTIVITY</strong> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Reactivity with Water</strong> -\nThe term \u201cNo reaction\u201d means that no hazard results when the chemical reacts or\nmixes with water.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Where a hazard does\nresult, it is described.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Reactivity with Common\nMaterials</strong> - This is limited to hazardous reactions with fuels and with common\nmaterials of construction such as metal, wood, plastics, cement, and\nglass.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The nature of the hazard, such as\nsevere corrosion or formation of a flammable gas, is described.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Stability During\nTransport</strong> - The term \u201cStable\u201d means that the chemical will not decompose in a\nhazardous manner under the conditions of temperature, pressure, and mechanical\nshock that are normally encountered during shipment; the term does not apply to\nfire situations.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Where there is a\npossibility of hazardous decomposition, an indication of the conditions and the\nnature of the hazard is given.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Neutralizing Agents for\nAcids and Caustics</strong> - In all cases involving accidental discharge, dilution with\nwater may be followed by use of the agent specified, particularly if the\nmaterial cannot be flushed away; the agent specified need not necessarily be\nused.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Polymerization </strong>- A few\nchemicals can undergo rapid polymerization to form sticky, resinous materials,\nwith the liberation of much heat.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The\ncontainers may explode.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>For these\nchemicals the conditions under which the reaction can occur are given.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Inhibitor of\nPolymerization</strong> - The chemical names and concentrations of inhibitors added by\nthe manufacturer to prevent polymerization are given.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong></span><strong>WATER POLLUTION<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Aquatic Toxicity</strong> - The\nform of data presentation used by the Environmental Protection Agency's \u201cOil\nand Hazardous Material-Technical Assistance Data System (OHM-TADS)\u201d is used\nhere.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Reading from left to right and\nseparated by slashes (/) are the following data:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Concentration in parts\nper million by weight (or milligrams per liter) at which the chemical was\ntested; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Time of exposure in\nhours;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Name of the aquatic\nspecies studied;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Effect observed; LC50\nmeans that approximately 50% of the fish will die under the conditions of\nconcentrations and time given.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>TLm\n(Median Tolerance Limit) means that approximately 50% of the fish will show\nabnormal behavior (including death) under the conditions of concentrations and\ntime given; the term EC50 (Effective Concentration50) is used sometimes instead\nof TLm;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The kind of water used\nin the test (fresh or salt)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Some chemicals have\nbeen tested with many species of fish.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Where the data were available, the </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">data sheet cites one\nillustrative test in fresh water and one in salt water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Waterfowl Toxicity</strong> -\nVery little information is available.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>In\na few cases there is entered the LD50 value, which indicates the dose (in\nmilligrams per kilogram of body weight) that is lethal to about half the\nwaterfowl tested.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Biological Oxygen\nDemand (BOD)</strong> - Also called \u201cbiochemical oxygen demand,\u201d this is a standard way\nof describing how much oxygen dissolved in water is consumed by biological\noxidation of the chemical during the stated period of time.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The unit lb/lb indicates the pounds of oxygen\nconsumed by each pound of chemical during the time stated.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>When given in percent, the values indicate\nthe pounds of oxygen consumed by each 100 pounds of chemical during the time\nstated.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If the percentage is followed by\n\u201c(theor.)\u201d, it indicates the pounds of oxygen theoretically required to completely\noxidize 100 pounds of the chemical.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Food Chain\nConcentration Potential</strong> - If the chemical is consumed by fish, marine plants,\nwaterfowl, etc., that are in turn eaten by other species, the substance may\naccumulate and ultimately be consumed by humans.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Where this occurs, an indication of the\npotential hazard and its significance is given.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>GESAMP Hazard Profile</strong> \u2013\nA composite list of hazard profiles evaluated by the Joint Group of Experts on\nthe Scientific Aspects of Marine Environmental Protection (GESAMP).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>A summary of the legends used in the profile\nfollows.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong>Bioaccumulation and\nTainting<o:p></o:p></strong></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">+<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Bioaccumulated to significant extent\nand known to produce a hazard to&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>aquatic\nlife or human health.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Z<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Bioaccumulated with attendant risk to\naquatic organisms or human<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>health,\nhowever, with short retention of the order of one week or less.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; </span>Non-hazardous\n(non-irritant, not a sensitizer)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">XXX<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Highly objectionable because of persistency,\nsmell or poisonous or irritant characteristics; as a result contaminated\nbeaches liable to be closed; also used when there is clear evidence that the\nsubstance is a human carcinogen or that the substance has the potential to\nproduce other serious specific long-term adverse health effects in humans.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">XX<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Moderately objectionable because of the\nabove characteristics, but short-term effects leading only to temporary\ninterference with use of beaches; also used when there is credible scientific\nevidence that the substance is an animal carcinogen but where there is no clear\nevidence to indicate that the material has caused cancer in humans, or when\nthere is evidence from laboratory studies that the substance could have the\npotential to produce other serious specific long-term adverse health effects.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;
