Yet\nour Italian waitress who rules India and her \u201cnot so bright\u201d son, thinks this is\nfanstasy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">INCA OF PERU is \u201c Child\nof the sun\u201d in Quechua . In Sanskrit Dinaka has same meaning. Dinakar is a\ncommon name in India.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">AZTEC OF MEXICO is\nderived from \"worshipper of Ashtabhuja or Ashtak ( 8 armed ) \" , the\neight armed God- found in Mexican temples.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">\n</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">No where in the word are multi-armed idols found, except in India.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FKd2pTDORJM/UA50xAkXVuI/AAAAAAAAN7Y/FKmMWDEx1po/s1600/AZTAC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FKd2pTDORJM/UA50xAkXVuI/AAAAAAAAN7Y/FKmMWDEx1po/s640/AZTAC.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Trilokinath, the Hindu\nruler of the three worlds, was known to the Mexicans by the name, until the\nSpanish conquerors mistakenly changed the name into Tloque Nahuaque. William\nMacLeod had written about the similarity between the Mexican volador ritual and\nthe Indian rite of hook-swinging.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-oliPbwL0cbs/Ui4gnPr2NlI/AAAAAAAAlu4/Awb5itQhaIw/s1600/56190_ganesha_azte_lg.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-oliPbwL0cbs/Ui4gnPr2NlI/AAAAAAAAlu4/Awb5itQhaIw/s640/56190_ganesha_azte_lg.gif\" width=\"339\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<i><span style=\"color: red;\">Above: Aztec Ganesha ( elephant god )</span></i><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">MAYANS OF GUATEMALA and\nYuacatan call Kundalini, as kultunlilni.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Kultunlilni is the vital life force empowering all human growth and\ndevelopment. This crucial life-force is the same as what is known in Hindu\ncosmology as the serpent power: Kundalini. In a temple in Guatemala is a statue\nof an incarnation of Vishnu as Kurma, the tortoise. The sculpture is richly and\nfinely detailed and strongly suggests that it can only be done by a pure Hindu\nIndian.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A wall panel (Panel No.\n3 of Temple 0-13, at Piedras Negras, Guatemala; reproduced as Plate 69, page\n343 of 'The Ancient Maya' by S.G. Morley) belonging to the Later Classic Stage\nof Mexican history, associated with the peaking of Maya architecture and\nsculpture. It depicts the Ramayana. The artistic design and postures of the\nfigures carved can be compared to those found at Ajanta and Ellora caves in\nIndia.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Mexicans throne is\nsame as the Hindu Simhasan (Lion throne).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>The Kings wore turbans and travelled in Indian palanquins.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4WlvmdG0Bmk/UA52slUajDI/AAAAAAAAN8I/RwqSpc4O4pE/s1600/imagesCAN2OUUC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4WlvmdG0Bmk/UA52slUajDI/AAAAAAAAN8I/RwqSpc4O4pE/s400/imagesCAN2OUUC.jpg\" width=\"265\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">US<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Ambassador Miles Poindexter, to Mexico, in\nhis two-volume 1930s treatise The Ayar-Incas called the Mayan civilization\n\"unquestionably Hindu.\" He said that that primitive Aryan words and\npeople came to South merica across the Pacific ocean . Poindexter gives a long\nlist of words of the Quichua languages and their analogous forms in Indian\nSanskrit. He also detailed the similarities between the hymns of the Inca\nrulers of Peru and Vedic hymns <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cKF9c3rYmQo/UA63oP9Ie1I/AAAAAAAAN_M/eUfUxd9_xkg/s1600/imagesCA8G0KQQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cKF9c3rYmQo/UA63oP9Ie1I/AAAAAAAAN_M/eUfUxd9_xkg/s1600/imagesCA8G0KQQ.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cLQKBrbdpIg/UA63szDgnxI/AAAAAAAAN_U/Ih6P1fgKPjQ/s1600/columbian.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"312\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cLQKBrbdpIg/UA63szDgnxI/AAAAAAAAN_U/Ih6P1fgKPjQ/s400/columbian.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Betel-chewing with lime\nand coca-whew and tobacco, as well as the gourd-container for the lime are\ncommon to both people. The Peruvian substitute for tobacco, which was used for\nmedicinal purposes, was a shrub, called cuca (coca).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mexican temples and\nidols, as in India, were lavishly decorated with gold and precious stones. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mayan gods Xiuhtechutli\nand Xipe Totec have their Vedic counterparts in Indra and Agni. Indra or\nXiuhtechutli, is the rain god and guardian of the Eastern Quadrant, and Agni,\nor Xipe Totec, is the god of sacrificial fire, born in wood and the life force\nof trees and plants.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Mayas had\nceremonies like Namakaranam, Punyaha vachana and Gurukula. They put their\nofferings to gods in water tanks like Hindus. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7MP-kGUdO5U/UA54rEApmgI/AAAAAAAAN9U/_vf-Iqery2I/s1600/imagesCAO30EM6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"310\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7MP-kGUdO5U/UA54rEApmgI/AAAAAAAAN9U/_vf-Iqery2I/s320/imagesCAO30EM6.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ships made in\nKerala never hugged the coast like European ships. These ships which could hold\nmore than thousand people did cross-ocean from South India to West coast of\nSouth America. Chinese traveller Fa Hein had written that he himself travelled\ncross-ocean with 500 others. These ships were made with aged Teak and Rosewood,\nthe best for shipbuilding.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Our ancient Jataka stories wrote about large Indian\nships carrying seven hundred people.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Brahmanda Purana provides the best and most detailed description of\nworld map drawn on a flat surface using an accurate scale. When Vasco da Gama\nlanded in Calicut ( my hometown ) in 1498, the King Zamorin, had whipped out a\nworld map and asked him where he came from,much to his surprise<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lord Ganesha is seen\nwith his vehicle rat in Inca mythology in Peru.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Lord Ganesha was found in temple of Diego Riviera in Mexico City.\nHanuman and Lord Shiva can be seen in the Guatemala Museum. Shiva Lingam was\nfound in Vera Cruz and in Mexico City. The Mexican Vishnu holds the traditional\nGadha or mace and his Chakra. The image of Vishnu\u2019s tortoise Kurma avatar\nincarnation is preserved by the United Fruit Line in the museum at Quiragua,\nGuatemala. They have named this image , the Turtle Stone. Indra and the Vamana\n(midget Brahmin ) avatar who did in Kerala ( my home state ) Asura King\nMahabali can be seen in the Mexican National Museum .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Maya Codex\nTro-Cortesianus shows a tortoise, a central churning rod and a serpent being\nused as a rope by figures of dark and light shade, which is the Hindu Samudhra\nManthan. The tortoise, is, however, on the summit of the mountain pestle\ninstead of being beneath it, and the other form of the serpent god appears\nabove his avatar. Round the mountain-pestle is twisted a snake. Two dark gods,\nevidently demonic forms of deities, like the Indian Asuras, hold one end of the\nsnake-rope while the other end is grasped by the elephant god Ganesha.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-neePfqAwAjA/UA52-c2ZFnI/AAAAAAAAN8Q/E-LVaCM5_V0/s1600/imagesCADEERZ6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-neePfqAwAjA/UA52-c2ZFnI/AAAAAAAAN8Q/E-LVaCM5_V0/s1600/imagesCADEERZ6.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The largest temple in\nMexico City was the temple of Lord Shiva, the War God of the Mexican whom the\nSpanish invaders found entwined by golden snakes. The Mexican temple had the\nGopuram South Indian temple MERU style.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sir Thomas Stamford\nBingley Raflles or the father of Singapore wrote,\u201dThe great Hindu temple of\nBorobudur might readily be mistaken for a Central American Temple. Every page\nof Peruvian poetry bears the imprint of Ramayana and Mahabharata.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mayan crystal skulls\ncould have been carved in ancient times without instruments and tools of today.\nThe most amazing thing was that the ancient skull weighing 5.13 kg, 203.4 mm\nlong and 125.4 mm wide had been made of a whole crystal. This fact contradicted\nthe laws of physics. The research by Hewlett-Packard in 1964 in a special\nlaboratory revealed that the skull had been made long before the first\ncivilizations appeared in that part of America where the skull was found. In\naddition, rock crystal of such perfect quality could not be found in that area.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-C5CE5nd6dX4/UA53VXqD1II/AAAAAAAAN8c/8VVPamjLL-I/s1600/COLN.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"419\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-C5CE5nd6dX4/UA53VXqD1II/AAAAAAAAN8c/8VVPamjLL-I/s640/COLN.png\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Crystal quartz is the\nsame material used in microchips that can hold billions of bits of information.\nGiven that, imagine the amount of info a whole skull can hold.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>These<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>13 Crystal Skulls are<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>linked to\nthe \u201cYear Zero\u201d or December 21, 2012, the date at which the Mayan Calendar\nends. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The rock crystal has a\nhardness that is slightly lower than that of topaz, corundum, and diamond; it\ncan be cut with diamonds only. It is astonishing, but the ancient Mayans\nmanaged to cut it somehow, and even made a lower jaw with the joints. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">Diamonds\nwere found only in India till 1886.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now let me get back to\nVaastu.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--mnlVdOH_ak/UA53uCSt57I/AAAAAAAAN8k/cZwIBlCBRk8/s1600/imagesCAHHUDDZ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"248\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/--mnlVdOH_ak/UA53uCSt57I/AAAAAAAAN8k/cZwIBlCBRk8/s320/imagesCAHHUDDZ.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mayans like Hindus\nworshiped the very concept of space, specifically a space made according to the\nmodular system. There is a sacred room in the center of the Chidambaram Siva\nTemple in South India, where space or akasha ( ether ) is worshiped- there is no\nidol. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The temple structure at\nthe top is exactly 1/4th of the base according to Vastu Vedic principles of\nMayan.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>The name of the structure is\nchilambalam, meaning a sacred space. Mayan chilambalam refers to a sacred space,\nas does Tamil Chidambaram. Yok'hah in Mayan means \"on top of\ntruth,\"<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>is what is<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>yoga in Sanskrit. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Machu Picchu temples\nand structures follows the Indian Vaastu. The layout of these structures,\nlocations for doors, windows, proportions of width to length, roof styles,\ndegree of slopes for roofs, column sizes, wall thicknesses, etc., all conform\ncompletely to the principles and guidelines as prescribed in the Vastu Shastras\nof Maya Danava in India. Residential layouts are identical to those found in\nMohenjodaro.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kMTp9B8-Oao/UA54BAQ8-NI/AAAAAAAAN8s/0bDg7O3fdd0/s1600/imagesCAR6PFBT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kMTp9B8-Oao/UA54BAQ8-NI/AAAAAAAAN8s/0bDg7O3fdd0/s400/imagesCAR6PFBT.jpg\" width=\"398\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The temple layouts are identical to those that he is building\ntoday and that can be found all over India.Maya Danava advocated the use of an\neight-by-eight square, for a total of 64 units, which is known as the Vastu\nPurusha Mandala. The buildings were oriented toward certain points of the\ncompass, also a principle of Maya, rather than randomly placed. Also the\nlengths of buildings were never more than twice their width, as Maya Danava\nstipulated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The sculptures were\nsimilar or identical to India, such as the earrings, ear plugs, teeth, head\ndresses, even buckles around the waist. There are bas reliefs of priests\nsitting in lotus posture meditating.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As in Mayan buildings,\nIndians have been using lime mortar for all of their stone and brick buildings.\nThis can been seen in the monumental creations in Mahabalipuram and also in the\nSouth Indian temples.. The outer surfaces were plastered, embellishments worked\nout in lime mortar, then painted.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The size of plots,\nposition of doors and windows, proportions, form of roofs, inclination angles\nof roofs, diameter of columns, width of walls etc. are perfectly in accordance\nwith the rules of Vaastu.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As per Vaastu , the\nbest location to build a temple is at a tirtha(holy place), which is<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>a ford or crossing place from this world to\nthe above-a point of marriage between transcendence and the mundane. A tirtha\nprovides a crossing place for the upward journey of the soul and a place for\nthe downward crossing-for the crossing of higher entities who sometimes descend\nto this world for the good of mankind. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In Indian architecture,\nthe dwelling is itself a shrine. A home is called manushyalaya, literally,\n\"human temple\". It is not merely a shelter for human beings in which\nto rest and eat. The concept behind house design is the same as for temple\ndesign, so sacred and spiritual are the two spaces. The \"open\ncourtyard\" system of house design was the national pattern in India before\nWestern models were introduced. The s is called Brahmasthanam, meaning the\n\"nuclear energy field\". It should be kept unbuilt and open to the sky\nso as to have contact with the outer space (akasha).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>The northeast quarter is called Isanya, the\nsoutheast Agni, the southwest Niruthi and northwest Vayu. These are said to\npossess the qualities of four respective devatas or gods\u2014Isa, Agni, Niruthi and\nVayu. Accordingly\u2014with due respect to ecological friendliness with the subtle\nforces of the spirit\u2014those spaces (quarters) are assigned as follows: northeast\nfor the home shrine, southeast for the kitchen, southwest for the master\nbedroom and northwest for the storage of grains.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Energy is primarily\nconsidered as emanating from the center of the building. It originates from\nsubtle earth energy called Vaastu Purusha and subtle cosmic energy (Unified\nField) called Vastu Purusha which meet in the center of the building and then\nspread outward in all directions. these two energies unite and form the five\nelements which then distribute in the for corner zones. This energy is a\nmixture of Vaastu energy, which is subtle energy from the earth, and Vastu\nenergy which is subtle energy from Consciousness itself.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-B0Ya6vL-9iw/UA55UIuqqmI/AAAAAAAAN9k/MyP5zYjR6tI/s1600/imagesCA0H8VN2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-B0Ya6vL-9iw/UA55UIuqqmI/AAAAAAAAN9k/MyP5zYjR6tI/s1600/imagesCA0H8VN2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Even my home is made as\nper principles of Vaastu. Let me quote a few among hundreds of rules.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only new material\nshould be used for the construction of the building.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dig a well in N-E direction and use this\nground water for the construction of the house.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One must paint his/her house in light colors\navoiding red and black for bringing prosperity.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Doors must be opened at\ninner side of the house not at outer side as it brings luck and positive energy\nin the house.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The guest room should be at the North-West\nside of the house and closer to the living room and at the front side of the\nhouse.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">While placing the bed\nmake sure that you do not sleep with your head to the north side as that will\ncreate a repelling magnetic force in your blood stream that will cause\ndisruption in sleep. You can sleep with you head towards any other side, but\nthe best side to keep your head while sleeping is south.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The safe should be\nplaced in south west side and it should be opened in the north direction. You\nneed to keep the north east side empty.</span></div>\nThe NE side of the plot ( kanni moola ) must be raised and kept free of garbage.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hMY8MCAzHaU/UA51B3O6ejI/AAAAAAAAN7g/_ig1puV4pfE/s1600/imagesVVNMM.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"248\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-hMY8MCAzHaU/UA51B3O6ejI/AAAAAAAAN7g/_ig1puV4pfE/s400/imagesVVNMM.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It must be noted that the Spanish grossly magnified and exaggerated the bad points of these great cultures (like human sacrifices). It was selective reporting and vested interpretation to paint them in bad light and to show that Christianity did them a great favour in converting them from uncouth pariahs to cultured humans.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the Spanish conquest, the first Bishop of Mexico, Juan de Zumarraga, burned all the records of the Library of Texcoco in Tlateloco market square as \"the work of the Devil,\" and religious fanatics destroyed temples and statues. Fray Diego de Landa, the second Bishop of Yucatan, following the pattern, reduced the Maya Library in Yucatan to ashes in 1562. Bishop Diego da Landa burnt a huge bonfire of valuable documents and nothing but the three codices of 'Chilam Balam' could survive the holocaust....<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"We found a large number of their books of these letters, and because they did not have anything in which there was not superstition and falsehoods of the devil, we burned them all, which they felt very sorry for and which caused them grief.\" <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It was Landa that gave the orders for all the Mayans to bring all manuscripts to the public squares in Mani to be burned. All these books contained what would now be priceless information on astronomy, medicine, religion, and philosophy. The burning of manuscripts continued for decades. Soldiers were encouraged to ransack palaces, public buildings, and private houses to find manuscripts. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Zi6SEgLcXyw/UA55aUEHGII/AAAAAAAAN9s/tUYD9ni8sWM/s1600/imagesCA3G2GV5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Zi6SEgLcXyw/UA55aUEHGII/AAAAAAAAN9s/tUYD9ni8sWM/s400/imagesCA3G2GV5.jpg\" width=\"328\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pablo Jose de Arriaga, the head of the Jesuit College in Peru, in almost unparalleled fanaticism, caused the systematic and wholesale destruction of all state archives, customs records, royal and imperial archives, codes of laws, temple archives, and historical records. This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; On the other hand, the axolotl retains it throughout its entire life, making it unique among vertebrates<br />\n<br />\nHumans have also been known to regenerate the tips of the fingers, including the bone and skin. I once lost the tip of my left forefinger on the ship--it has regrown fully.<br />\n<br />\nBECAUSE OF CHEMICAL POLLUTION FOR TANNERIES, GANGES MACROPHAGES HAVE LOST THEIR ANCIENT POWERS OF REGENERATION..<br />\n<br />\nInjecting a drug to get rid of macrophages in an axolotl\u2019s limb before amputation leads to the accumulation of scar tissue instead of regrowth..<br />\n<br />\nThis scarring, which happens when a protein called collagen becomes disordered, is a normal part of wound healing in humans, but it is unusual in axolotls. This result suggests that macrophages are essential for regeneration<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls stay 'babies' for their whole lives. Axolotls are neotenic creatures meaning they achieve sexual maturity without losing any of their larval features<br />\n<br />\nIf an axolotl is given a shot of iodine, it will experience a rush of hormones that triggers the animal's growth processes, and it will \"grow up\" and resemble a mature tiger salamander, their closest relative.<br />\n<br />\nHowever, this is not the axolotl's natural state. \"Grown-up\" axolotls are typically listless and die about a year after the injection.<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls can regenerate pretty much any body part. A number of amphibians are capable of regenerating limbs, but axolotls take this habit up a notch by regenerating jaws, spinal cords, skin and even portions of their brain. Axolotls can also receive organ transplants and will not reject the new organ.<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls have a genome 10 times the size of the human genome..<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B0GJOjfYn74</span><br />\n<br />\ncapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_72MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_72MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\n<br />\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_70B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 16px 0px 8px;\"><div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c1061350286957344881\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_70M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/17821568266464145690\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">CK</a></cite><span class=\"icon user\" style=\"font-weight: bold;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/08/comments-overflow-for-inoperative-load.html?showComment=1535398556183#c1061350286957344881\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">August 28, 2018 at 1:05 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_70MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px;\">\nPranam Captain Ajit,<br />\nSir if water has memory, and Axolotls have such phenomenal regenerative superpowers, then the water had this imprinted within, making it \"holier\" in its power than the Ganga waters.<br />\nAlso, is it correct to assume Danavas were closer to Mayans and Aztecs than Vedics of the later period.
